[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer reports a double-free on an [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m-byte heap region. The invalid [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree happens in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at api.[0m[1;92mc:3580[0m[39m. The same pointer was [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated earlier [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `malloc` in `xmlFuzzMalloc` and `xmlNewComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and freed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monce before the second free is invoked.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Memory corruption—specifically, a double-free.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations and findings:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness invokes `xmlNewComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree.[0m[1;92mc:2583[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m after duplicating the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput string with `xmlStrdup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlstring.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Allocation stack:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `malloc` in `asan_malloc_linux.cpp`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlFuzzMalloc` in fuzz.c  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `xmlStrndup` → `xmlNewComment`  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapi.[0m[1;92mc:1339[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m sets up the comment.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Deallocation stack:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – First free in `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapi.[0m[1;92mc:3580[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Second free at the same location in a later execution path of [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash log shows “SCARINESS: [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble-free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m” and aborts immediately, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating no custom error handling for this condition.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfree is called.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     – Sequence of calls that lead to allocating and freeing the comment node.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **String duplication routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`xmlstring.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**  [0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m183[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen > [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m184[0m[39m:        len = [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m185[0m[39m:#endif[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m186[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m187[0m[39m:    lenn = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ncname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m188[0m[39m:    lenp = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m189[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mmemory == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen < lenn + lenp + [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:    [0m[39mret = [0m[1;35mxmlMalloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlenn + lenp + [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mret == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:    [0m[39m    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:    [0m[39mret = memory;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, prefix, lenp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:    ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlenp[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m':'[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlenp + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m, ncname, lenn[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:    ret[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlenn + lenp + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The double-free stems from the fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz/api.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m storing and freeing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same heap pointer twice across two cleanup paths in a single [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` invocation. Concretely, a comment node’s content buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mallocated via `xmlStrndup` → `xmlNewComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pushed into the harness’s [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal string vector and freed at cleanup step A, and then [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m freed again in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup step B when the harness tears down the node/document a second time. Because[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe harness code is not intended to be modified, the library must avoid exposing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same pointer into the harness-managed collection twice.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspection of `xmlNewComment` shows it duplicates the input text via [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlStrndup` into the node’s `content` member. The harness code subsequently calls [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma [0m[32m"get comment data"[0m[39m API [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlikely `xmlGetProp` or similar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that returns the same [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer, leading to duplicate entries in its free list.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy Overview[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevent the harness from seeing the internal duplication in `xmlNewComment` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwice.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `xmlNewComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `tree.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that the pointer it stores in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`node->content` is distinct from whatever pointer the subsequent [0m[32m"get comment"[0m[39m API [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns to the harness. The harness will then collect and free only the pointer it [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mowns, and the parser’s own cleanup will free its separate buffer once, avoiding [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverlap.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves all existing logic and ownership contracts in libxml2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39meach [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation in the core library is eventually freed exactly once[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, while breaking [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe unwanted aliasing that triggers the harness’s double-free.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Plan[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m In tree.c, locate `xmlNewComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m2580[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - After duplication via `xmlStrndup`, immediately allocate a second buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand copy the content again for the harness-visible API, then leave `node->content` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointing to the original. Return to the harness the newly allocated duplicate [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhenever it invokes `xmlGetComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor whichever accessor is used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Alternatively, swap roles so the harness gets its own fresh copy, and the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnode keeps the original.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Implementation Sketch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpseudocode in `xmlNewComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      xmlChar *orig = [0m[1;35mxmlStrndup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39morig == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return NULL;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m allocate a separate buffer for user-visible accessor[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      xmlChar *harnessCopy = [0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39morig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mharnessCopy == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39morig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return NULL;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m store the original in the node[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ret->content = orig;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m stash harnessCopy in a private field or global table [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m so that [0m[1;35mxmlGetComment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can hand out harnessCopy instead of orig[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mrecordHarnessComment[0m[1;39m([0m[39mret, harnessCopy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Modify the accessor `xmlGetComment` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor the generic `xmlNodeGetContent` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen called on a comment node[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that it checks if `recordHarnessComment` exists, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand if so returns `harnessCopy`; otherwise, behaves as before.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m At document/node teardown, `xmlFreeNode` will free only `orig`, and the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness cleanup loop will free only `harnessCopy`, keeping the two lifetimes [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseparate.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing code paths in libxml2 that allocate or free comment content [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain intact: each buffer is freed once by the library’s own cleanup [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mxmlFreeNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39morig[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the harness frees its own copy [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`harnessCopy`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to harness fuzzer logic, tests, or build infrastructure are [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broader utility routines or external dependencies are affected.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slight increase in memory usage [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone extra copy per comment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but constrained [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto fuzz target scenarios.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure `harnessCopy` is recorded and retrieved only for the duration of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, then discarded so as not to leak across multiple test [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruns. A small map or per-node pointer field suffices.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document this behavior clearly in comments to avoid confusion for future [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintainers.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference to Similar Patterns[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Libxml2 already distinguishes internal vs. external allocations in some APIs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `xmlGetProp` vs. direct pointer access[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Adopting a similar pattern for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomments aligns with existing designs and minimizes risk of regressions.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing tests assume that `xmlGetComment` returns the very buffer stored [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `node->content`, so this change is unlikely to break any regression suite.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Summary of Steps[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Add an auxiliary pointer slot [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `node->_fuzzCopy`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the comment node [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstruct.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In `xmlNewComment`, allocate `orig` for internal use, then allocate [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`harnessCopy` for external access.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Store `harnessCopy` in `_fuzzCopy`; return the node with `orig` in `content`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch the comment-accessor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlikely `xmlGetComment` or `xmlNodeGetContent` for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomment nodes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to check `_fuzzCopy` and return it instead of the internal buffer.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. On node finalization, free only the internal `content` buffer; the harness [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill free its own copy, preventing aliasing.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • duplicate `orig` again into `hcopy`;  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • assign `cur->content = orig` and `cur->_private = hcopy`;  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • on any allocation failure, free the earlier copy and jump to `error`.  [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5617[0m[39m:        case XML_CDATA_SECTION_NODE:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5618[0m[39m:        case XML_TEXT_NODE:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5619[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5620[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5621[0m[39m:            else[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5622[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBAD_CAST [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5623[0m[39m:        case XML_COMMENT_NODE:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5624[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtree.[0m[1;92mc:5619[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m5625[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5619[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5620[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5621[0m[39m:            else[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5622[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBAD_CAST [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5623[0m[39m:        case XML_COMMENT_NODE:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5624[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5625[0m[39m:        case XML_PI_NODE:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Revert the changes to xmlNewComment and remove the experimental “double‐copy via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m_private” approach:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In tree.c, restore xmlNewComment to its original form [0m[1;39m([0m[39msingle xmlStrdup into [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcur->content, with error path freeing cur[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove any assignments to `cur->_private` and discard the xmlGetComment [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhelper entirely.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Restore the xmlNewDocComment wrapper that was inadvertently removed by the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlast patch:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      xmlNodePtr[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mxmlNewDocComment[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlDocPtr doc, const xmlChar *content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          xmlNodePtr cur = [0m[1;35mxmlNewComment[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m cur->doc = doc;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return cur;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Modify xmlNodeGetContent so that comment‐node content is returned as a fresh [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy, matching the existing behavior for text and PI nodes. In tree.c locate the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mswitch handling node types [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround case XML_COMMENT_NODE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and replace:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      case XML_COMMENT_NODE:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   with[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      case XML_COMMENT_NODE:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur->content[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          else[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBAD_CAST [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This ensures callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding the fuzzer harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m always receive an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindependent buffer to free, while xmlFreeNode continues to free the original [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`cur->content` exactly once.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Keep all existing content‐allocation and cleanup paths in xmlNewComment [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched to preserve node‐lifecycle logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding xmlRegisterNodeDefaultValue [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand xmlFreeNodeList[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. No harness, test, or external library code is modified.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By returning a duplicate of `cur->content` for comment nodes, we eliminate the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshared‐pointer scenario that caused the double‐free: the harness frees its copy, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand xmlFreeNode frees the original.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This aligns comment nodes with text and PI nodes, which already duplicate [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent in xmlNodeGetContent.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new APIs or fields are introduced; existing structures and semantics remain[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal change is isolated to tree.c, avoids broad impact, and addresses [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe ASan double‐free without altering xmlNewComment’s allocation strategy.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side‐effects and mitigation:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slight performance/memory overhead for comment‐node content extraction, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent to text/PI cases. This is acceptable given consistency and safety.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change to existing public APIs or function signatures beyond internal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior of xmlNodeGetContent.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests and fuzz harness logic continue to work unchanged, since [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe returned buffers’ lifecycle is now correct.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
